Unfortunately, I could not get strace working. At all. I got the cygwin version working but my linux terminal just sucks.
I also forgot my cpsc password so could not run this on the servers. Sorry.
Therefore, I have to guess on why one's faster instead of looking at the results.

In the times I ran it, the cpp version was faster ( 2 runs are provided below). This could be because the .sh
script spent significantly longer in kernel mode. This also (may) signify more system calls, as 
you don't need to spend time in kernel mode unless you're doing system calls. I suspect
actually running strace successfully would reflect these results. 

Why would the results be different? For one, c++ code needs to be compiled to run on a computer.
The compiler is also written by people way smarter than me, who write it in ways to optimize 
resource usage. Minimizing system calls would definitely be one way to optimize. 
I'm not entirely sure how bash scripts are run, e.g. if they are compiled.
